 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">Introduction. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">This Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> is being filed in connection with the completion on April&#160;1, 2020 (the &#8220;Closing Date&#8221;) of the previously announced business combination between <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> US, Inc., a Delaware corporation <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#8220;T-Mobile&#8221;),</span> and Sprint Corporation, a Delaware corporation (&#8220;Sprint&#8221;), pursuant to the Business Combination Agreement, dated as of April&#160;29, 2018 (as amended, the &#8220;Business Combination Agreement&#8221;), by and among <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> Sprint, Huron Merger Sub LLC, a Delaware limited liability company and a wholly owned subsidiary of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> (&#8220;Merger Company&#8221;), Superior Merger Sub Corporation, a Delaware corporation and a wholly owned subsidiary of Merger Company (&#8220;Merger Sub&#8221;), Starburst I, Inc., a Delaware corporation (&#8220;Starburst&#8221;), Galaxy Investment Holdings, Inc., a Delaware corporation (&#8220;Galaxy&#8221; and, together with Starburst, the &#8220;SoftBank US HoldCos&#8221;), and for the limited purposes set forth therein, Deutsche Telekom AG, an <span style="font-style:Italic">Aktiengesellschaft</span> organized and existing under the laws of the Federal Republic of Germany (&#8220;Deutsche Telekom&#8221;), Deutsche Telekom Holding B.V., a <span style="font-style:Italic">besloten vennootschap met beperkte aansprakelijkheid</span> organized and existing under the laws of the Netherlands (&#8220;DT Holding&#8221;), and SoftBank Group Corp., a Japanese <span style="font-style:Italic">kabushiki kaisha</span> (&#8220;SoftBank&#8221;). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Pursuant to the Business Combination Agreement, on the Closing Date, (i)&#160;the SoftBank US HoldCos merged with and into Merger Company, with Merger Company continuing as the surviving entity and as a wholly owned subsidiary of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> (the &#8220;HoldCo Mergers&#8221;), and (ii)&#160;immediately following the HoldCo Mergers, Merger Sub merged with and into Sprint, with Sprint continuing as the surviving corporation and as a wholly owned indirect subsidiary of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> (the &#8220;Merger&#8221; and, together with the HoldCo Mergers, the &#8220;Merger Transactions&#8221;). In connection with the completion of the Merger Transactions, the parties to the Business Combination Agreement waived the condition to closing set forth in the Business Combination Agreement with respect to the final&#32;consent of the California Public Utilities Commission (the &#8220;CPUC&#8221;), to the extent required, such that all regulatory approvals required for the Merger Transactions to be completed on April&#160;1, 2020 were satisfied or waived as of such date.&#160;The parties entered into this waiver without any admission as to whether such final consent was required in connection with the Merger Transactions, following the release of the CPUC&#8217;s proposed decision to approve the Merger on March&#160;11, 2020. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Pursuant to the Business Combination Agreement, (i)&#160;at the effective time of the HoldCo Mergers, all the issued and outstanding shares of common stock of Galaxy, par value $0.01 per share, and all the issued and outstanding shares of common stock of Starburst, par value $0.01 per share, held by SoftBank Group Capital Limited, a private limited company incorporated in England and Wales and a wholly owned subsidiary of SoftBank and the sole stockholder of each of Galaxy and Starburst (&#8220;SoftBank UK&#8221;), were converted such that SoftBank UK received an aggregate number of shares of common stock, par value $0.00001 per share, of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span>&#32;<span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#8220;T-Mobile</span> Common Stock&#8221;), equal to the product of (x) 0.10256 (the &#8220;Exchange Ratio&#8221;) and (y)&#160;the aggregate number of shares of common stock, par value $0.01 per share, of Sprint (&#8220;Sprint Common Stock&#8221;), held by the SoftBank US HoldCos, collectively, immediately prior to the effective time of the HoldCo Mergers, and (ii)&#160;at the effective time of the Merger (the &#8220;Effective Time&#8221;), each share of Sprint Common Stock issued and outstanding immediately prior to the Effective Time (other than shares of Sprint Common Stock held by Merger Company or held by Sprint as treasury stock) were converted into the right to receive a number of shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock equal to the Exchange Ratio. No fractional shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock will be issued in connection with the Merger Transactions. Each holder of </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">Sprint Common Stock converted pursuant to the Merger Transactions who would otherwise have been entitled to receive a fraction of a share of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock (after taking into account all shares held by such holder) will instead receive cash (without interest) in lieu of such fractional share in accordance with the terms of the Business Combination Agreement. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">In addition, immediately following the Effective Time on the Closing Date, pursuant to the Letter Agreement, dated as of February&#160;20, 2020 (the &#8220;Letter Agreement&#8221;), by and among <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> SoftBank and Deutsche Telekom, SoftBank UK surrendered to <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> for no additional consideration, an aggregate of 48,751,557 shares (the &#8220;SoftBank Specified Shares Amount&#8221;) of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile </span>&#32;Common Stock (the &#8220;SoftBank Disposition&#8221;). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Letter Agreement further provides that if the trailing <span style="white-space:nowrap">45-day</span> volume-weighted average price per share of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock on the NASDAQ Global Select Market (the &#8220;NASDAQ&#8221;) is equal to or greater than $150.00 at any time during the period commencing on the second anniversary of the Closing Date and ending on December&#160;31, 2025, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will issue to SoftBank, for no additional consideration, a number of shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock equal to the SoftBank Specified Shares Amount (the &#8220;Additional Shares&#8221;), subject to the terms and conditions set forth in the Letter Agreement. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">As of immediately following the Merger Transactions and after giving effect to the SoftBank Disposition, Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank held approximately 43% and 24%, respectively, of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock, with the remaining approximately 33% of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock held by public stockholders, in each case on a fully diluted basis. The <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock continues to trade on the NASDAQ under the ticker symbol &#8220;TMUS&#8221;. As further described in this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> and in <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> other periodic reports filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;SEC&#8221;), Deutsche Telekom is also a holder of a portion of the outstanding debt of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA, Inc., a Delaware corporation <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#8220;T-Mobile</span> USA&#8221;). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The description of the Merger Transactions and the SoftBank Disposition contained in this Introduction does not purport to be complete and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the Business Combination Agreement, which is filed as Exhibit 2.1 hereto, Amendment No.&#160;1, dated as of July&#160;26, 2019, to the Business Combination Agreement, which is filed as Exhibit 2.2 hereto, Amendment No.&#160;2, dated as of February&#160;20, 2020, to the Business Combination Agreement, which is filed as Exhibit 2.3 hereto, and the Letter Agreement, which is filed as Exhibit 10.1 hereto. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The total aggregate consideration payable in the Merger Transactions was approximately 379&#160;million shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock after giving effect to the SoftBank Disposition. The issuance of shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock in connection with the Merger Transactions was registered under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (the &#8220;Securities Act&#8221;), pursuant to a registration statement on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">S-4</span> (File No.<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;333-226435)</span> filed by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> with the SEC and declared effective on October&#160;29, 2018 (the &#8220;Registration Statement&#8221;). The joint consent statement/prospectus included in the Registration Statement contains additional information about the Business Combination Agreement and the Merger Transactions. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>

<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;1.01 </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Pursuant to the Business Combination Agreement, on April&#160;1, 2020, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank entered into an amendment and restatement (the &#8220;Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement&#8221;) of the Stockholder&#8217;s Agreement, dated as of April&#160;30, 2013, by and between <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and Deutsche Telekom. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement includes provisions setting forth the rights of Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank to designate individuals to be nominees for election to <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> board of directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) and any committees thereof. Pursuant to the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement, at all times when Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank beneficially own at least 50% of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock and any other securities of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> that are entitled to vote in the election of directors (collectively, <span style="white-space:nowrap">&#8220;T-Mobile</span> Voting Securities&#8221;) in the aggregate and any such <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Voting Security continues to be subject to the Proxy (as defined below), (i) the Board will consist of a total of 14 directors, (ii)&#160;each of Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank (except, in the case of SoftBank, if it beneficially owns less than a certain minimum percentage of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile </span>&#32;Voting Securities (10% if the condition giving rise to SoftBank&#8217;s right to the Additional Shares has been satisfied, or 9% if it has not)) has the right to designate a specified number of nominees for election to the Board in accordance with the terms of the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement, subject to certain requirements, including requirements with respect to the &#8220;independence&#8221; of certain nominees under applicable stock exchange listing standards and rules of the SEC, (iii)&#160;the chairperson of the Board will be a Deutsche Telekom designee and (iv)&#160;the Board will have certain committees, which committees will be comprised in the manner specified in the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement. The Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement further provides that at all times when Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank beneficially own less than 50% of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Voting Securities in the aggregate or no <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Voting Security continues to be subject to the Proxy, then, in each case, each of Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank has the right to designate a number of nominees for election to the Board equal to the percentage of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile </span>&#32;Voting Stock that it beneficially owns (provided that such percentage is 10% or more) multiplied by the number of directors on the Board, rounded to the nearest whole number greater than zero. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Based on the percentages of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock beneficially owned by Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank as of immediately following the Merger Transactions and after giving effect to the SoftBank Disposition, under the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement, Deutsche Telekom has the right to designate nine individuals to be nominees for election to the Board and SoftBank has the right to designate four individuals to be nominees for election to the Board. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">In accordance with the terms of the Business Combination Agreement and the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement, as modified by certain transitional arrangements agreed to between the parties as described under Item 5.02 below, as of immediately following the Effective Time, the Board consists of a total of 14 directors, including nine directors designated by Deutsche Telekom, three directors designated by SoftBank, and each of John J. Legere (who will not be deemed to be a designee of Deutsche Telekom or of SoftBank for purposes of the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement) and G. Michael Sievert. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">In addition, pursuant to the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement and the Restated Charter, (i)&#160;as long as Deutsche Telekom beneficially owns 30% or more of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Voting Securities, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will not take certain actions without Deutsche Telekom&#8217;s prior written consent, including (a)&#160;incurring indebtedness above certain levels based on a </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">specified debt to cash flow ratio, (b)&#160;taking any action that would cause a default under any instrument evidencing indebtedness of Deutsche Telekom or its affiliates, (c)&#160;acquiring or disposing of assets or entering into mergers or similar acquisitions in excess of $1.0&#160;billion, (d)&#160;changing the size of the Board, (e)&#160;subject to certain exceptions, issuing equity of 10% or more of the then-outstanding shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock, or issuing equity to redeem debt held by Deutsche Telekom, (f)&#160;repurchasing or redeeming equity securities or making any extraordinary or <span style="white-space:nowrap">in-kind</span> dividend other than on a pro rata basis, or (g)&#160;making certain changes involving the Chief Executive Officer of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> and (ii)&#160;as long as SoftBank beneficially owns 22.5% or more of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Voting Securities, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will not take certain actions without SoftBank&#8217;s prior written consent, including (a)&#160;acquiring or disposing of assets or entering into mergers or similar acquisitions in excess of $1.0&#160;billion (other than a Sale of the Company (as defined in the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement), for which the prior written consent of SoftBank will not be required, but for which SoftBank has a match right as set forth in the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement) or (b)&#160;subject to certain exceptions, issuing equity of 10% or more of the then-outstanding shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock. <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile </span>&#32;has also agreed not to amend its certificate of incorporation and bylaws in any manner that could adversely affect Deutsche Telekom&#8217;s or SoftBank&#8217;s rights under the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement for as long as the applicable stockholder beneficially owns 5% or more of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Voting Securities. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Pursuant to the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement, Deutsche Telekom, SoftBank and their respective affiliates are generally prohibited from acquiring <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Voting Securities that would cause their collective beneficial ownership to exceed 80.1% of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Voting Securities unless such acquiring stockholder makes an offer to acquire all of the then-remaining outstanding shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock at the same price and on the same terms and conditions as the proposed acquisition from all other stockholders of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> which is either (i)&#160;accepted or approved by a majority of the directors on the Board, which majority includes a majority of the directors who are not affiliated with Deutsche Telekom or SoftBank under the terms of the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement (the &#8220;Required Approval&#8221;), or (ii)&#160;accepted or approved by holders (other than Deutsche Telekom, SoftBank and their respective affiliates) of a majority of the shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock (other than shares held by Deutsche Telekom, SoftBank and their respective affiliates). Each of Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank is also prohibited from transferring any shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock in any transaction that would result in the transferee owning more than 30% of the outstanding shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock unless the transfer is approved by the Board (including the Required Approval) or the transferee offers to acquire all of the then outstanding shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock at the same price and on the same terms and conditions as the proposed transfer. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">So long as SoftBank beneficially owns 22.5% or more of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Voting Securities, the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement also provides SoftBank with a match right in connection with a possible sale of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> (whether initiated by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> or a third party). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement sets forth certain additional rights and obligations of each of Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank, including information rights, registration rights and <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-competition</span> restrictions. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">The foregoing summary of the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement does not purport to be complete and is subject to, and qualified in its entirety by, the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement, which is filed as Exhibit 10.2 hereto. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Proxy Agreement </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Pursuant to the Business Combination Agreement, on April&#160;1, 2020, Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank entered into a Proxy, <span style="white-space:nowrap">Lock-up </span>&#32;and ROFR Agreement (the &#8220;Proxy Agreement&#8221;). The Proxy Agreement establishes between Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank certain rights and obligations in respect of the shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock owned by each of Deutsche Telekom, SoftBank and certain of their respective affiliates to enable Deutsche Telekom to consolidate <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> into Deutsche Telekom&#8217;s financial statements following the completion of the Merger Transactions. Pursuant to the Proxy Agreement, at any meeting of the stockholders of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> the shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock beneficially owned by SoftBank will be voted in the manner directed by Deutsche Telekom (the &#8220;Proxy&#8221;), which obligation will terminate upon the earliest of: (i)&#160;with respect to each such share of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock, the date on which such share is transferred to a third party in accordance with the terms of the Proxy Agreement, subject to certain exceptions, (ii)&#160;the date on which Deutsche Telekom owns 55% or more of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Voting Securities and (iii)&#160;the date on which Deutsche Telekom has transferred an aggregate number of shares representing 5% or more of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock as of immediately following the Effective Time. The Proxy Agreement also contains certain restrictions on the ability of each of SoftBank and Deutsche Telekom to transfer or acquire shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock, including that each of SoftBank and Deutsche Telekom is not permitted to transfer its shares without the prior written consent of the other stockholder from and after the Effective Time until the fourth anniversary of the Effective Time, subject to certain exceptions, including for transfers of up to 5% of the <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock outstanding as of the Effective Time beginning after the first anniversary of the Effective Time and up to an additional 10% of the <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock outstanding as of the Effective Time beginning after the second anniversary of the Effective Time. As a result of the Proxy Agreement, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> continues to be a &#8220;controlled company&#8221; for purposes of NASDAQ rules, which provides <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> with exemptions from certain corporate governance requirements under NASDAQ rules. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The foregoing description of the Proxy Agreement is not complete and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the Business Combination Agreement, which is filed as Exhibit 2.1 hereto, the form of Proxy Agreement attached as Exhibit F to the Business Combination Agreement, and Amendment No.&#160;2, dated as of February&#160;20, 2020, to the Business Combination Agreement, which is filed as Exhibit 2.3 hereto. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">License Agreement Amendment </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Pursuant to the Business Combination Agreement, on April&#160;1, 2020, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and Deutsche Telekom entered into an amendment (the &#8220;License Agreement Amendment&#8221;) to the License Agreement, dated as of April&#160;30, 2013 (the &#8220;License Agreement&#8221;), by and between <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and Deutsche Telekom. The License Agreement Amendment provides, among other things, that the license fee payable by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> to Deutsche Telekom under the License Agreement will be subject to a cap of $80.0&#160;million per year through December&#160;31, 2028.</p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>

<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;1.02 </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Termination of a Material Definitive Agreement.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Existing Deutsche Telekom Credit Facilities </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On the Closing Date, in connection with the Merger Transactions and pursuant to the Financing Matters Agreement, dated as of April&#160;29, 2018 (the &#8220;Financing Matters Agreement&#8221;), by and between <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and Deutsche Telekom, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA repaid all outstanding amounts owed under, and terminated, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s existing $4.0&#160;billion Term Loan Credit Agreement, dated as of November&#160;9, 2015 and as amended from time to time, by and among <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA, as borrower, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> as a guarantor, the subsidiary guarantors party thereto, Deutsche Bank AG New York Branch (&#8220;DB&#8221;), as administrative agent, and Deutsche Telekom, as lender. Further, on the Closing Date, pursuant to the Financing Matters Agreement, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA terminated (i)<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s existing Secured Revolving Credit Agreement, dated as of December&#160;29, 2016 and as amended from time to time, by and among <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA, as borrower, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> as a guarantor, the subsidiary guarantors party thereto and Deutsche Telekom, as administrative agent and lender, and (ii)<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s existing Unsecured Revolving Credit Agreement, dated as of December&#160;29, 2016 and as amended from time to time, by and among <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA, as borrower, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> as a guarantor, the subsidiary guarantors party thereto and Deutsche Telekom, as administrative agent and lender. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Notes held by Deutsche Telekom </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On the Closing Date, in connection with the Merger Transactions and pursuant to the Financing Matters Agreement, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA purchased from Deutsche Telekom the outstanding $2,000,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s 5.300% Senior Notes due 2021 and the outstanding $2,000,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s 6.000% Senior Notes due 2024, in each case at a price equal to par plus accrued and unpaid interest on such notes to, but not including, the Closing Date. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">As disclosed in <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> filed on December&#160;21, 2018, amendments to the Indenture, dated as of April&#160;28, 2013 (as amended and supplemented, the &#8220;Indenture&#8221;), by and among <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA, the guarantors party thereto and Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas, governing certain other <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA notes held by Deutsche Telekom, became effective immediately prior to the completion of the Merger Transactions. These amendments pertain to <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s 4.000% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2022-1,</span> 5.125% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2025-1,</span> 5.375% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2027-1,</span> 4.500% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2026-1</span> and 4.750% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2028-1</span> (collectively, the &#8220;DT Notes&#8221;). These amendments, among other things, amend the Indenture (i)&#160;pertaining to all DT Notes to allow certain entities related to Sprint&#8217;s existing spectrum securitization notes program (the &#8220;Sprint Spectrum Note Facility&#8221;) to be <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-guarantor</span> restricted subsidiaries under the Indenture, provided that the aggregate principal amount of the notes issued and outstanding under the Sprint Spectrum Note Facility does not exceed $7.0&#160;billion and provided that the principal amount of such notes shall reduce the amount available under the ratio basket with respect to Credit Facilities (as defined in the Indenture), (ii) pertaining to the 5.125% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2025-1</span> to amend the maturity date </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">from April&#160;15, 2025 to April&#160;15, 2021, (iii) pertaining to the 5.375% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2027-1</span> to amend the maturity date from April&#160;15, 2027 to April&#160;15, 2022 and (iv)&#160;pertaining to the 5.125% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2025-1</span> to provide that <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA shall be required to redeem 100% of the then-outstanding 5.125% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2025-1,</span> at a price equal to 100% of the aggregate principal amount of the 5.125% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2025-1,</span> plus accrued and unpaid interest on the 5.125% Senior Notes due <span style="white-space:nowrap">2025-1</span> redeemed to, but not including, the applicable redemption date, on any date that <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA redeems or prepays any other notes or debt securities (other than the other DT Notes) issued by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and outstanding as of April&#160;29, 2018. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">As of immediately following the Merger Transactions and after giving effect to the SoftBank Disposition, Deutsche Telekom held approximately 43% of the outstanding <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock on a fully diluted basis. Deutsche Telekom is a holder of a portion of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s outstanding debt, as further described in this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> and in <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> other periodic reports filed with the SEC. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>

<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;2.01 </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Completion of Acquisition or Disposition of Assets.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">The information set forth in the Introduction regarding the acquisition of the equity interests of Sprint is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;2.03 </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Creation of a Direct Financial Obligation or an Obligation under an <span style="white-space:nowrap">Off-Balance</span> Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">New Credit Agreement </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On the Closing Date, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA entered into a Credit Agreement (the &#8220;New Credit Agreement&#8221;) by and among <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA, as borrower, DB, as administrative agent, and the lenders and other financial institutions party thereto, providing for a $4.0&#160;billion term loan facility (the &#8220;New Term Loan Facility&#8221;) and a $4.0&#160;billion revolving credit facility (the &#8220;New Revolving Credit Facility&#8221;). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The loans under the New Term Loan Facility mature on April&#160;1, 2027. The loans under the New Term Loan Facility are payable in quarterly installments of 0.25% of the sum of the aggregate amount of the term loans outstanding thereunder on the Closing Date, with the remaining balance due at maturity, except as otherwise extended or replaced. The loans under the New Term Loan Facility may be prepaid by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA at any time without penalty or premium, subject to customary LIBOR breakage provisions and a soft call prepayment premium of 1.00% of the outstanding principal amount of the loans under the New Term Loan Facility payable upon the refinancings of certain loans by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA with lower priced debt prior to October&#160;1, 2020, subject to customary exclusions. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Commitments under the New Revolving Credit Facility will mature on April&#160;1, 2025, except as otherwise extended or replaced. <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA may repay amounts borrowed, reborrow and/or terminate the commitments under the New Revolving Credit Facility (in whole or part) at any time without premium or penalty. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The rates of interest on amounts borrowed under the Term Loan Facility are based on, at <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s option, either LIBOR (subject to a 0% LIBOR floor) plus a margin of 3.00% or an alternate base rate plus a margin of 2.00%, and amounts borrowed under the Revolving Credit Facility are based on, at <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s option, either LIBOR (subject to a 0% LIBOR floor) </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">plus a margin of 1.25% or an alternate base rate plus a margin of 0.25%, with the margins subject to reduction to 1.00% and 0.00%, respectively, if <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Total First Lien Net Leverage Ratio (as defined in the New Credit Agreement) is less than or equal to 0.75 to 1.00. The alternate base rate is the highest of (i)&#160;the prime rate of the administrative agent, (ii)&#160;the federal funds effective rate plus 0.50% and (iii)<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;one-month</span> adjusted LIBOR plus 1.00%. In the event that LIBOR becomes unascertainable, is no longer made available or a public announcement has been made that it will no longer be available or syndicated loans are being executed or amended to incorporate or adopt a new benchmark to replace LIBOR, then <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and the administrative agent are permitted to amend the New Credit Agreement to replace LIBOR with an alternative benchmark rate. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The commitment fee for the New Revolving Credit Facility is 0.375% per annum, subject to reduction to 0.25% if <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Total First Lien Net Leverage Ratio is less than or equal to 0.75 to 1.00 and an increase to 0.50% if <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Total First Lien Net Leverage Ratio is greater than 1.25 to 1.00, in each case determined on a Pro Forma Basis (as defined in the New Credit Agreement) as of the last day of the most recently ended Test Period (as defined in the New Credit Agreement). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt"> <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s obligations under the New Credit Agreement are guaranteed by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and by all of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s wholly-owned domestic restricted subsidiaries (other than certain excluded subsidiaries including certain designated special purpose finance vehicle entities, insurance subsidiaries and immaterial subsidiaries), all of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> subsidiaries that guarantee certain of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile </span>&#32;USA&#8217;s indebtedness, and any subsidiary of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> that directly or indirectly owns any of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s equity interests. In addition, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s obligations under the New Credit Agreement and the guarantee obligations of the guarantors are supported by a first priority pledge (subject to permitted liens under the New Credit Agreement) in substantially all of the tangible and intangible personal property assets of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and the guarantors, in each case subject to certain exceptions as set forth in the New Credit Agreement, the Collateral Agreement, dated as of April&#160;1, 2020 (the &#8220;Collateral Agreement&#8221;), by and among <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and the other grantors party thereto in favor of Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas, as collateral trustee, and related documentation. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The New Term Loan Facility requires <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA to prepay outstanding term loans with (i)&#160;beginning with the fiscal year ending December&#160;31, 2021, a variable percentage of excess cash flow, ranging from 50% to 0% depending on <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s Total First Lien Net Leverage Ratio from time to time, (ii)&#160;a variable percentage, ranging from 100% to 50% depending on <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s Total First Lien Net Leverage Ratio, determined on a Pro Forma Basis as of the last day of the most recently ended Test Period, of the net cash proceeds in excess of (on an aggregate basis) $250.0&#160;million of certain asset sales by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA or any of its restricted subsidiaries (subject to certain reinvestment rights), and (iii) 100% of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s and its restricted subsidiaries&#8217; net cash proceeds from issuances, offerings or placements of debt obligations not permitted under the New Credit Agreement, in each case subject to certain exceptions set forth in the New Credit Agreement and related documentation. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The New Credit Agreement contains certain limitations on <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and its restricted subsidiaries with respect to dividends and other distributions, restrictions on investments, indebtedness and guarantees, sales of certain assets, affiliate transactions, liens, business activities and consolidations and mergers. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">The New Credit Agreement provides that <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA has the right at any time to request incremental term loans or incremental revolving credit commitments (or incremental equivalent debt) up to the greater of the sum of (a)&#160;the greater of (x) $11.0&#160;billion and (y) 50% of Consolidated Cash Flow (as defined in the New Credit Agreement) determined on a Pro Forma Basis for the most recently ended Test Period plus (b)&#160;the amount of all voluntary prepayments, cash amounts actually paid in connection with below-par term loan buybacks (to the extent such loans are cancelled) and undrawn commitment reductions of term loans, revolving credit loans, incremental term loans, incremental revolving credit loans and incremental equivalent debt (in each case (A)&#160;with respect to revolving credit loans, to the extent accompanied by a permanent reduction in such revolving credit commitments and (B)&#160;to the extent not funded with the proceeds of debt constituting &#8220;long-term debt&#8221; (other than debt in respect of any revolving credit facility)) plus (c)&#160;such other amount so long as such amount at such time could be incurred without causing <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s pro forma Total First Lien Net Leverage Ratio to exceed 2.0 to 1.0 in the case of incremental loans or commitments that are first lien obligations, Total Secured Net Leverage Ratio (as defined in the New Credit Agreement) to exceed 2.5 to 1.0 in the case of incremental loans or commitments that are junior lien obligations, Total Net Leverage Ratio (as defined in the New Credit Agreement) to exceed 6.0 to 1.0 in the case of incremental loans or commitments that are unsecured indebtedness or, in the case of incremental term loans incurred in connection with a permitted acquisition or other investment, the Total First Lien Net Leverage Ratio, Total Secured Net Leverage Ratio or Total Net Leverage Ratio, as applicable, immediately prior to such permitted acquisition or other investment. The lenders are not under any obligation to provide any such incremental commitments or loans. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The New Revolving Credit Facility contains a financial maintenance covenant, requiring <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA to maintain a Total First Lien Net Leverage Ratio of 3.30 to 1.00 or less at each fiscal quarter end beginning with the fiscal quarter ending September&#160;30, 2020. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The New Credit Agreement contains customary events of default, including, without limitation, payment defaults, covenant defaults, breaches of certain representations and warranties, cross defaults to certain material indebtedness, certain events of bankruptcy and insolvency, material judgments, a change of control coupled with a ratings downgrade, certain ERISA events and the invalidity of security documents and guarantees. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Bridge Term Loan Credit Agreement </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On the Closing Date, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA entered into a Bridge Term Loan Credit Agreement (the &#8220;Bridge Credit Agreement&#8221;) by and among <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA, as borrower, Goldman Sachs Bank USA, as administrative agent, and the lenders and other financial institutions party thereto, providing for a $19.0&#160;billion term loan facility. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The loans under the Bridge Credit Agreement, which were drawn on the Closing Date, mature 364 days following the Closing Date, which date of maturity may be extended by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA up to two times for an additional period of 182 days per extension, in each case subject to an extension fee of 0.25% of the aggregate principal amount of the loans outstanding on the date of such extension. The loans under the Bridge Credit Agreement are due at maturity (subject to extension as described in the preceding sentence). The loans under the Bridge Credit Agreement may be prepaid by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA at any time without penalty or premium, subject to customary LIBOR breakage provisions. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">The rates of interest on amounts borrowed under the Bridge Credit Agreement are based on, at <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s option, either LIBOR (subject to a 0% LIBOR floor) plus a margin of 1.25% or an alternate base rate, plus a margin of 0.25%, in each case, increasing by (a) 0.25% on the date falling on the last day of the three-month period following the Closing Date and (b)&#160;an additional 0.25% on the last day of the three-month period thereafter. The alternate base rate is the highest of (i)&#160;the prime rate of the administrative agent, (ii)&#160;the federal funds effective rate plus 0.50% and (iii)<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;one-month</span> adjusted LIBOR plus 1.00%. In the event that LIBOR becomes unascertainable, is no longer made available or a public announcement has been made that it will no longer be available or syndicated loans are being executed or amended to incorporate or adopt a new benchmark to replace LIBOR, then <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and the administrative agent are permitted to amend the Credit Agreement to replace LIBOR with an alternative benchmark rate. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Bridge Credit Agreement is subject to a duration fee on the aggregate principal amount of the loans then outstanding of (i) 0.50% payable on each of the 90th, 180th, 270th and 364th day after the Closing Date, and (ii) 0.75% payable on each of the 454th, 544th and 634th day after the Closing Date. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt"> <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s obligations under the Bridge Credit Agreement are guaranteed by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and by all of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s wholly-owned domestic restricted subsidiaries (other than certain excluded subsidiaries including certain designated special purpose finance vehicle entities, insurance subsidiaries and immaterial subsidiaries), all of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> subsidiaries that guarantee certain of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile </span>&#32;USA&#8217;s indebtedness, and any subsidiary of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> that directly or indirectly owns any of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s equity interests. In addition, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA&#8217;s obligations under the Bridge Credit Agreement and the guarantee obligations of the guarantors are supported by a first priority pledge (subject to permitted liens under the Bridge Credit Agreement) in substantially all of the tangible and intangible personal property assets of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and the guarantors, in each case subject to certain exceptions as set forth in the Bridge Credit Agreement, the Collateral Agreement and related documentation. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Bridge Credit Agreement requires <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA to prepay outstanding term loans with (i) 100% of the net cash proceeds of certain asset sales by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA or any of its restricted subsidiaries and (ii) 100% of the net cash proceeds of certain issuances, offerings or placements of debt obligations by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA or any of its restricted subsidiaries, in each case subject to an aggregate threshold of $1.0&#160;billion and certain other exceptions set forth in the Bridge Credit Agreement and related documentation. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Bridge Credit Agreement contains certain limitations on <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and its restricted subsidiaries with respect to liens and consolidations and mergers. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Bridge Credit Agreement contains customary events of default, including, without limitation, payment defaults, covenant defaults, breaches of certain representations and warranties, cross payment defaults and cross accelerations to certain material indebtedness, certain events of bankruptcy and insolvency, material judgments, a change of control coupled with a ratings downgrade, certain ERISA events and the invalidity of security documents and guarantees. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">Sprint Capital Corporation Notes </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On the Closing Date, pursuant to the Fifth Supplemental Indenture, dated as of April&#160;1, 2020 (the &#8220;Fifth Supplemental Indenture&#8221;), by and among Sprint Capital Corporation, Sprint Communications, Inc., <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span>&#32;<span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as trustee, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA guaranteed all obligations of Sprint Capital Corporation under Sprint Capital Corporation&#8217;s outstanding $2,475,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of 6.875% Senior Notes due 2028 and $2,000,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of 8.750% Senior Notes due 2032 (collectively, the &#8220;SCC Notes.&#8221;). The SCC Notes are Sprint Capital Corporation&#8217;s unsecured obligations and are also guaranteed on a senior unsecured basis by Sprint and Sprint Communications, Inc. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The SCC Notes were issued pursuant to an indenture, dated as of October&#160;1, 1998 (as amended and supplemented the &#8220;SCC Indenture&#8221;), by and among Sprint Capital Corporation, Sprint and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as successor to Bank One, N.A., as trustee. The SCC Indenture contains covenants and other terms, including covenants that, among other things, restrict the ability of Sprint and its restricted subsidiaries to create liens or other encumbrances, and merge, consolidate or sell, or otherwise dispose of, substantially all of their assets. The SCC Indenture, as so amended and supplemented, also contains customary events of default. These covenants and events of default are subject to a number of important qualifications and exceptions. Sprint Capital Corporation may, at its option, redeem some or all of the SCC Notes at any time at a specified &#8220;make-whole&#8221; redemption price plus accrued and unpaid interest to, but not including, the redemption date. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Sprint Communications, Inc. Notes </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On the Closing Date, pursuant to the Sixteenth Supplemental Indenture, dated as of April&#160;1, 2020 (the &#8220;Sixteenth Supplemental Indenture&#8221;), by and among Sprint Communications, Inc., <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span>&#32;<span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as trustee, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA guaranteed all obligations of Sprint Communications, Inc. under Sprint Communications, Inc.&#8217;s outstanding $1,500,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of 7.000% Senior Notes due 2020, $1,000,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of 11.500% Senior Notes due 2021 and $2,280,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of 6.000% Senior Notes due 2022 (collectively, the &#8220;SCI Notes&#8221;). The SCI Notes are Sprint Communications, Inc.&#8217;s unsecured obligations and are also guaranteed on a senior unsecured basis by Sprint. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The SCI Notes were issued pursuant to an indenture, dated as of November&#160;20, 2006 (as amended and supplemented, the &#8220;SCI Indenture&#8221;), by and between Sprint Communications, Inc. (formerly known as Sprint Nextel Corporation) and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as successor to The Bank of New York Trust Company, N.A., as trustee. The SCI Indenture contains covenants and other terms, including covenants that, among other things, restrict the ability of Sprint and its restricted subsidiaries to create liens or other encumbrances, and merge, consolidate or sell, or otherwise dispose of, substantially all of their assets. The SCI Indenture, as so amended and supplemented, also contains customary events of default. These covenants and events of default are subject to a number of important qualifications and exceptions. Sprint Communications, Inc. may, at its option, redeem some or all of the SCI Notes at any time at a specified &#8220;make-whole&#8221; redemption price plus accrued and unpaid interest to, but not including, the redemption date. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">Sprint Corporation Notes </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On the Closing Date, pursuant to the Seventh Supplemental Indenture, dated as of April&#160;1, 2020 (the &#8220;Seventh Supplemental Indenture&#8221;), by and among Sprint, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span>&#32;<span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as trustee, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA guaranteed all obligations of Sprint under Sprint&#8217;s outstanding $2,250,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of 7.250% Notes due 2021, $4,250,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of 7.875% Notes due 2023, $2,500,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of 7.125% Notes due 2024, $1,500,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of 7.625% Notes due 2025 and $1,500,000,000 in aggregate principal amount of 7.625% Notes due 2026 (collectively, the &#8220;Sprint Notes&#8221;). The Sprint Notes are Sprint&#8217;s unsecured obligations and are guaranteed on a senior unsecured basis by Sprint Communications, Inc. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Sprint Notes were issued pursuant to an indenture, dated as of September&#160;11, 2013 (as amended and supplemented, the &#8220;Sprint Indenture&#8221;), by and between Sprint and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as trustee. The Sprint Indenture contains covenants and other terms, including covenants that, among other things, restrict the ability of Sprint and its restricted subsidiaries to create liens or other encumbrances, and merge, consolidate or sell, or otherwise dispose of, substantially all of their assets. The Sprint Indenture, as so amended and supplemented, also contains customary events of default. These covenants and events of default are subject to a number of important qualifications and exceptions. Sprint may, at its option, redeem some or all of the Sprint Notes at any time at a specified &#8220;make-whole&#8221; redemption price plus accrued and unpaid interest to, but not including, the redemption date. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Spectrum Lease </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On the Closing Date, pursuant to a guarantee assumption agreement, dated as of April&#160;1, 2020, by and among Sprint Spectrum License Holder, LLC, Sprint Spectrum License Holder II LLC, Sprint Spectrum License Holder III LLC, T-Mobile, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and certain subsidiary guarantors, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span>&#32;<span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA and certain subsidiaries of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA guaranteed on a secured basis (with such security capped at $3.5 billion) the lease payment obligations of Sprint Communications, Inc. under an intercompany spectrum lease (the &#8220;Sprint Spectrum Lease&#8221;), which lease payments are used to service the indebtedness under spectrum-backed notes issued through a group of bankruptcy-remote special purpose entities under the Sprint Spectrum Note Facility. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Currently outstanding under the Sprint Spectrum Note Facility are $1,312,500,000 of Series <span style="white-space:nowrap">2016-1</span> 3.360% Senior Secured Notes, Class<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;A-1,</span> $2,100,000,000 of Series <span style="white-space:nowrap">2018-1</span> 4.738% Senior Secured Notes, Class<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;A-1</span> and $1,837,500,000 of Series <span style="white-space:nowrap">2018-1</span> 5.152% Senior Secured Notes, Class<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;A-2</span> (collectively, the &#8220;Sprint Spectrum-Backed Notes&#8221;), which were issued through a group of bankruptcy-remote special purpose entities (the &#8220;Sprint Spectrum Note Entities&#8221;) formed for such transaction, each of which, effective upon the completion of the Merger Transactions, are wholly-owned by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-guarantor</span> restricted subsidiaries under the <span style="white-space:nowrap">pre-existing</span>&#32;<span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> USA unsecured notes and the New Credit Agreement and the Bridge Credit Agreement. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Sprint Spectrum-Backed Notes are secured primarily by a separate pool of 2.5 GHz and 1.9 GHz spectrum, which has been pledged to secure indebtedness available under the Sprint </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">Spectrum Note Facility. Additional credit enhancement includes a letter of credit supporting an <span style="white-space:nowrap">18-month</span> interest and expense reserve and a pledge of the secured payment obligations under the Sprint Spectrum Lease. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Series <span style="white-space:nowrap">2016-1</span> 3.360% Senior Secured Notes, Class<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;A-1</span> were initially paid with interest-only payments from December 2016 through September 2017, followed by amortizing quarterly principal payments from December 2017 through September 2021. The Series <span style="white-space:nowrap">2018-1</span> 4.738% Senior Secured Notes, Class<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;A-1</span> are initially paid with interest-only payments from June 2018 through March 2021, followed by amortizing quarterly principal payments from June 2021 through March 2025. The Series <span style="white-space:nowrap">2018-1</span> 5.152% Senior Secured Notes, Class<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;A-2</span> are initially paid with interest-only payments from June 2018 through March 2023, followed by amortizing quarterly principal payments from June 2023 through March 2028. The issuers may optionally prepay the outstanding principal amount of all or any tranche of the Sprint Spectrum-Backed Notes in whole on any business day or in part on any payment date, without any obligation to prepay the Sprint Spectrum-Backed Notes of another series or tranche proportionately or otherwise, at a price equal to 100% of the aggregate principal amount of the Sprint Spectrum-Backed Notes prepaid plus accrued and unpaid interest, if any, to the applicable prepayment date, plus, in the case of any such optional prepayment at any time before the date that is one year prior to the anticipated repayment date (September 20, 2021 with respect to the Series <span style="white-space:nowrap">2016-1</span> 3.360% Senior Secured Notes, Class<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;A-1,</span> March&#160;20, 2025 with respect to the Series <span style="white-space:nowrap">2018-1</span> 4.738% Senior Secured Notes, Class<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;A-1</span> and March&#160;20, 2028 with respect to the Series <span style="white-space:nowrap">2018-1</span> 5.152% Senior Secured Notes, Class<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;A-2),</span> a specified &#8220;make-whole&#8221; prepayment premium. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">As the Sprint Spectrum Note Entities are wholly-owned subsidiaries of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> following the Merger Transactions, these entities will be consolidated and all intercompany activity will be eliminated for accounting purposes. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>

Legere and G. Michael Sievert. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">Resignation of Director </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On March&#160;26, 2020, in connection with the transactions contemplated by the Business Combination Agreement, Bruno Jacobfeuerborn submitted his resignation from his position as a director of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> effective as of the Effective Time. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Continued Service of Directors; Election of Directors </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">The nine directors designated by Deutsche Telekom pursuant to the Business Combination Agreement and the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement, each of whom previously served, and continues to serve, as a member of the Board, effective from and after the Effective Time are as follows: Timotheus H&#246;ttges (as Chairperson), Srikant Madhav Datar, Srini Gopalan, Lawrence H. Guffey, Dr.&#160;Christian&#160;P. Illek, Raphael K&#252;bler, Thorsten Langheim, Teresa A. Taylor and Kelvin R. Westbrook. Each of Mr.&#160;Datar, Mr.&#160;Guffey, Ms.&#160;Taylor and Mr.&#160;Westbrook is an independent director under the listing standards of NASDAQ. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The three directors designated by SoftBank pursuant to the Business Combination Agreement and the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement, each of whom was appointed by the Board to fill the vacancies resulting from the resignation of the individual referred to above and the increase in the size of the Board referred to above, in each case effective from and after the Effective Time, are as follows: Marcelo Claure, Stephen Kappes and Ronald Fisher. Mr.&#160;Claure currently serves as Executive Vice President and Chief Operating Officer of SoftBank. He formerly served as Executive Chairman of Sprint. Mr.&#160;Fisher currently serves as Vice Chairman of the board of directors of SoftBank. He formerly served as Vice Chairman of the board of directors of Sprint. Mr.&#160;Kappes also previously served as a director of Sprint. It is anticipated that one additional director will be designated by SoftBank, and appointed by the Board, following the Closing, such that, effective from and after such time, SoftBank will have four designees on the Board, in accordance with the terms of the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement. Each of Mr.&#160;Kappes and the director to be designated by SoftBank following the Closing is (or will be, as applicable) an independent director under the listing standards of NASDAQ. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">CEO Transition </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">As described below, the Board has named Mr.&#160;Sievert to succeed Mr.&#160;Legere as Chief Executive Officer of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> effective as of immediately following the Closing. In connection with the foregoing transition, the parties to the Business Combination Agreement have entered into a waiver pursuant to which Mr.&#160;Legere will continue to serve as a member of the Board from and after the Effective Time until the date of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> 2020 annual meeting of stockholders. From and after such date, in accordance with the terms of the Business Combination Agreement and the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement, the Board will consist of a total of 14 directors, including nine directors designated by Deutsche Telekom, four directors designated by SoftBank and the Chief Executive Officer of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile. </span></p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Board Committees </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">In accordance with the terms of the Business Combination Agreement and the Amended and Restated Stockholders&#8217; Agreement, the Board established a CEO Selection Committee and a Transaction Committee, and appointed directors to serve on each such committee and its other standing committees, in each case effective as of the Effective Time, as follows: </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>

The remaining committee assignments, if any, of the director to be designated by SoftBank following the completion of the Merger Transactions have not yet been determined. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Amendments to Executive Employment Arrangements </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On March 26, 2020, the Board adopted (i)&#160;a second amendment to the amended and restated employment agreement, dated April&#160;1, 2017, with John J. Legere (the &#8220;Legere Amendment&#8221;), and (ii)&#160;a first amendment to the employment agreement, dated November&#160;15, 2019, with G. Michael Sievert (the &#8220;Sievert Amendment&#8221;). The material terms of the Legere Amendment and the Sievert Amendment are described below. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Legere Amendment </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">The Legere Amendment amended Mr.&#160;Legere&#8217;s employment agreement to provide that he would continue to serve as <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s </span>&#32;Chief Executive Officer through the earlier of (i)&#160;immediately following the Closing and (ii)&#160;April&#160;30, 2020 (the earlier such time or date, the &#8220;Termination Date&#8221;). Pursuant to the Legere Amendment, Mr.&#160;Legere&#8217;s employment with <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> automatically terminated as of the Termination Date; however, pursuant to certain transitional arrangements agreed to between the parties to the Business Combination Agreement as described above, Mr.&#160;Legere continues to serve as a member of the Board through the date of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> 2020 annual meeting of stockholders. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Pursuant to the Legere Amendment, for purposes of determining the number of performance-based restricted stock units held by Mr.&#160;Legere that become earned and vested based on <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> total shareholder return relative to its peer group in connection with Mr.&#160;Legere&#8217;s termination of employment on the Termination Date, (i)&#160;Sprint will be excluded from <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> peer group, (ii)<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> and its peer group companies&#8217; stock price will be measured based on the average closing prices for the <span style="white-space:nowrap">30-day</span> period ending on the last trading day immediately prior to the Termination Date, and (iii)&#160;any conditions to the accelerated vesting of Mr.&#160;Legere&#8217;s Incremental PRSUs and <span style="white-space:nowrap">True-Up</span> PRSUs (each as defined in his employment agreement) will be deemed satisfied. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">The Legere Amendment also amended the severance benefits that Mr.&#160;Legere is, subject to his timely execution and <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-revocation</span> of a release of claims in favor of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> eligible to receive upon his termination of employment due to the expiration of the employment term on the Termination Date to provide that, in lieu of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> paying for or reimbursing (as applicable) an exclusive office and exclusive executive assistant for 18 months (at up to $25,000 per month) following termination, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will pay Mr.&#160;Legere a lump sum amount equal to $450,000. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Legere Amendment also provides that <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will pay or reimburse Mr.&#160;Legere for the reasonable costs and expenses incurred by him in connection with the collection of his personal belongings from <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Bellevue, Washington offices and the winding up of his affairs in the greater Bellevue, Washington area. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The foregoing description of the Legere Amendment is qualified in its entirety by the full text of the Legere Amendment, a copy of which will subsequently be filed with the SEC. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Sievert Amendment </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">The Sievert Amendment amended Mr.&#160;Sievert&#8217;s employment agreement to provide that he would continue to serve as <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s </span>&#32;President and Chief Operating Officer through the earlier of (i)&#160;immediately following the Closing and (ii)&#160;April&#160;30, 2020 (the earlier such time or date, the &#8220;CEO Start Date&#8221;). Mr.&#160;Sievert now serves as <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> President and Chief Executive Officer, effective as of the CEO Start Date. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The foregoing description of the Sievert Amendment is qualified in its entirety by the full text of the Sievert Amendment, a copy of which will subsequently be filed with the SEC. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>
