any Person that will be a successor to the Company, whether by merger, consolidation or sale of all or substantially all of its assets, and (c)&nbsp;each Stockholder may assign certain of its rights in accordance with Section&nbsp;5.11. Any
purported direct or indirect assignment in violation of this Section&nbsp;7.2 shall be null and void <I>ab initio</I>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Section&nbsp;7.3
<U>Amendments; Waiver</U>. No amendment, modification or discharge of this Agreement, and no waiver hereunder, and no extension of time for the performance of any of the obligations hereunder, shall be valid or binding unless set forth in writing
and duly executed by the parties. Any such waiver shall constitute a waiver only with respect to the specific matter described in such writing and shall in no way impair the rights of any party granting any waiver in any other respect or at any
other time. The waiver by the Company or any Stockholder of a breach of, or a default under, any of the provisions hereof, or to exercise any right or privilege hereunder, shall not be construed as a waiver of any other breach or default of a
similar nature, or as a waiver of any of such provisions, rights or privileges hereunder. Except as expressly provided in this Agreement, the rights and remedies herein provided are cumulative and none is exclusive of any other, or of any rights or
remedies that any party may otherwise have at law or in equity. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Section&nbsp;7.4 <U>Termination</U>. Except as otherwise provided in this
Agreement (including Section&nbsp;5.6(b)), this Agreement shall terminate with respect to any particular Stockholder at any time after which such Stockholder&#146;s Voting Percentage is less than 5%; <U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that
(a)&nbsp;the obligations of the Company under Section&nbsp;3.2(a) shall terminate on the DT Specified Actions Termination Date, and the obligations of the Company under Section 3.2(b) shall terminate on the SoftBank Specified Actions Termination
Date; (b)&nbsp;the indemnity and contribution provisions contained in Section&nbsp;5.9 and Section&nbsp;5.10 shall remain operative and in full force and effect regardless of any termination of this Agreement; and (c)&nbsp;the provisions of Article
VI and this Article VII shall survive any termination of this Agreement or any provision thereof. Nothing in this Agreement shall be deemed to release any party from any liability for any willful and material breach of this Agreement occurring prior
to any termination hereof or to impair the right of a party to compel specific performance by the other party of its obligations under this Agreement. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Section&nbsp;7.6 <U>Governing Law; Jurisdiction; Forum; Waiver of Trial by Jury</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) THIS AGREEMENT SHALL BE GOVERNED BY AND CONSTRUED IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE LAWS OF THE STATE OF DELAWARE, REGARDLESS OF THE LAWS THAT MIGHT
OTHERWISE GOVERN UNDER ANY APPLICABLE PRINCIPLES OF CONFLICTS OF LAWS THEREOF. In any action between the parties arising out of or relating to this Agreement, each of the parties (i)&nbsp;irrevocably and unconditionally consents and submits to the
exclusive jurisdiction and venue of the Court of Chancery of the State of Delaware in and for New Castle County, Delaware, (ii)&nbsp;agrees that it will not attempt to deny or defeat such jurisdiction by motion or other request for leave from such
court, and (iii)&nbsp;agrees that it will not bring any such action in any court other than the Court of Chancery for the State of Delaware in and for New Castle County, Delaware, or, if (and only if) such court finds it lacks subject matter
jurisdiction, the federal court of the United States of America sitting in the State of Delaware, and appellate courts thereof, or, if (and only if) each of such Court of Chancery for the State of Delaware and such federal court finds it lacks
subject matter jurisdiction, any state court within the State of Delaware. Service of process, summons, notice or document to any party&#146;s address and in the manner set forth in Section&nbsp;7.5 shall be effective service of process for any such
action. Each party hereto irrevocably designates C.T. Corporation as its agent and attorney in fact for the acceptance of service of process and making an appearance on its behalf in any such claim or proceeding and for the taking of all such acts
as may be necessary or appropriate in order to confer jurisdiction over it before the aforementioned courts and each party hereto stipulates that such consent and appointment is irrevocable and coupled with in interest. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) EACH PARTY ACKNOWLEDGES AND AGREES THAT ANY CONTROVERSY WHICH MAY ARISE UNDER THIS AGREEMENT IS LIKELY TO INVOLVE COMPLICATED AND
DIFFICULT ISSUES, AND THEREFORE IT HEREBY IRREVOCABLY AND UNCONDITIONALLY WAIVES, TO THE FULLEST EXTENT PERMITTED BY APPLICABLE LAW, ANY RIGHT IT MAY HAVE TO A TRIAL BY JURY IN RESPECT OF ANY LITIGATION DIRECTLY OR INDIRECTLY ARISING OUT OF OR
RELATING TO THIS AGREEMENT AND ANY OF THE AGREEMENTS DELIVERED IN CONNECTION HEREWITH OR THE TRANSACTIONS CONTEMPLATED HEREBY OR THEREBY. EACH PARTY CERTIFIES AND ACKNOWLEDGES THAT (i)&nbsp;NO REPRESENTATIVE, AGENT OR ATTORNEY OF ANY OTHER PARTY HAS
REPRESENTED, EXPRESSLY OR OTHERWISE, THAT SUCH OTHER PARTY WOULD </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-45- </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Section&nbsp;7.8 <U>Entire Agreement; No Other Representations</U>. This Agreement and the Business Combination Agreement and, with respect to

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Section&nbsp;7.10 <U>Severability</U>. If any term or other provision of this Agreement is invalid, illegal or incapable of being enforced by
any rule of law or public policy, all other conditions and provisions of this Agreement shall nevertheless remain in full force and effect. Upon a determination that any term or other provision is invalid, illegal or incapable of being enforced, the
parties hereto shall negotiate in good faith to modify this Agreement so as to effect the original intent of the parties as closely as possible to the fullest extent permitted by applicable Law in an acceptable manner to the end that the
transactions contemplated hereby are fulfilled to the extent possible<U>.</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Section&nbsp;7.11 <U>Counterparts</U>. This Agreement may
be executed in two or more counterparts, all of which shall be considered one and the same agreement and shall become effective when one or more counterparts have been signed by each of the parties hereto and delivered to the other parties. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Section&nbsp;7.12 <U>Affiliated Entities</U>. To the extent that any Controlled Affiliate of DT is a DT Stockholder, DT shall cause such

Annex I, and to execute any and all documents or instruments and take such other actions required, or otherwise </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
reasonably requested by SoftBank, to ensure that such Controlled Affiliate is subject to the obligations under this Agreement applicable to the DT Stockholder (<U>provided</U> that any failure to
execute such documents or instruments or take such other actions shall not affect such obligations hereunder). To the extent that any Controlled Affiliate of SoftBank is a SoftBank Stockholder, SoftBank shall cause such Controlled Affiliate to
comply with all obligations under this Agreement applicable to the SoftBank Stockholder, and in furtherance of the foregoing, if any Controlled Affiliate of SoftBank becomes a Beneficial Owner of Voting Securities on or after the date hereof, such
Controlled Affiliate shall, and SoftBank shall cause such Controlled Affiliate to, promptly (and in advance of such Controlled Affiliate becoming a Beneficial Owner, if reasonably practicable) execute a joinder in substantially in the form of Annex
I, and to execute any and all documents or instruments and take such other actions required, or otherwise reasonably requested by DT, to ensure that such Controlled Affiliate is subject to the obligations under this Agreement applicable to the
SoftBank Stockholder (<U>provided</U> that any failure to execute such documents or instruments or take such other actions shall not affect such obligations hereunder). </P>

terms used but not defined in this Joinder shall have the respective meanings ascribed to such terms in the Stockholders&#146; Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">By executing and delivering this Joinder to the Stockholders&#146; Agreement, the undersigned hereby adopts and approves the
Stockholders&#146; Agreement and agrees, effective commencing on the date hereof and as a condition to the undersigned becoming a Beneficial Owner of Voting Securities, to become a party to, and to be bound by and comply with the provisions of, the
Stockholders&#146; Agreement applicable to the [DT][SoftBank] Stockholder in the same manner as if the undersigned were an original signatory to the Stockholders&#146; Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The undersigned hereby represents and warrants that it is a Controlled Affiliate of [DT][SoftBank]. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Article VII of the Stockholders&#146; Agreement is hereby incorporated herein by reference, <I>mutatis mutandis</I>. </P>

and Sprint shall combine in one or more transactions in accordance with the Business Combination Agreement (the &#147;<B>Proposed Transaction</B>&#148;). </P>

&#147;<B>Agreement</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Agreement requires in Section&nbsp;7.4 that the Parties meet after five years to attempt to
agree on a New License Fee to be applicable as of January&nbsp;1, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Parties have met and agreed on a New License Fee
that will be the License Fee for the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ten-year</FONT> period commencing January&nbsp;1, 2019; provided, however, that the agreed New Licensee Fee will terminate and be of no further effect if the Proposed Transaction
fails to close according to the terms of the Business Combination Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">NOW THEREFORE, in consideration of covenants and agreements
contained herein, and other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which is hereby acknowledged, DT and Licensee agree as follows: </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">
December&nbsp;31, 2028, will be determined in accordance with the Agreement without any application of the benchmark, accountant or arbitration processes or proceedings described in Sections 7.4
and 7.5. The New License Fee for the five-year period from January&nbsp;1, 2029, through December&nbsp;31, 2033, and thereafter for subsequent five-year renewal terms, will be as negotiated by the Parties or, if they fail to reach agreement on the
New License Fee for any such renewal terms, by application of the accountant or arbitration proceedings described in Sections 7.4 and 7.5 of the Agreement without application of the Cap. For the avoidance of doubt, the Cap shall apply to any New
License Fee in accordance with the Agreement for the two five-year renewal terms from January&nbsp;1, 2019 through December&nbsp;31, 2028. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">6. <B>Recitals.</B> The Recitals set forth above are material to this Amendment and are a part hereof. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">7. <B>Effectiveness</B>. This Amendment shall become effective as of the Amendment Effective Date. The License Fee for calendar year 2018
shall be determined in accordance with the Agreement without any application of Sections 7.4 and 7.5. If the Business Combination Agreement is terminated, the new Section&nbsp;7.6 provided above will terminate and be of no force or effect as of the
date of such termination, and the New License Fee shall be determined as provided in Section&nbsp;7.4 and applied retroactively to January&nbsp;1, 2019. In such event, Licensee shall pay any difference between what it has paid through such date and
what it owes due to the retroactive application of the New License Fee within 60 days after receipt of a DT issued proper invoice complying with the applicable tax laws. Except as may be amended hereby, the Agreement shall continue in full force and
effect as written. The Agreement, as amended and supplemented by this Amendment, shall be read, taken and construed as one and the same instrument. To the extent that any term of the Agreement (prior to its amendment hereby) conflicts with any term
of this Amendment as set forth herein after the Amendment Effective Date, the terms of this Amendment shall control to the extent of such conflict. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">8. <B>Counterparts</B>. This Amendment may be executed in counterparts, each of which, when executed, shall be deemed to be an original and
all of which together will be deemed to be one and the same instrument. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the parties hereto have executed this Amendment effective as
of the Amendment Effective Date. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Completes Merger with Sprint to Create the New
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Supercharged <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> positioned to
deliver unparalleled network reliability, value, innovation and commitment to customers now, when it&#146;s more important than ever </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>CEO transition occurs with close of merger; John Legere hands off CEO role to Mike Sievert </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Bellevue, Washington and Overland Park, Kansas &#151; April</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;1, 2020 </B>&#151; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc.
(NASDAQ: TMUS) announced today that it has officially completed its merger with Sprint Corporation to create the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> a supercharged <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> that will
deliver a transformative 5G network. The parent of the combined company is <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc., whose shares of common stock will continue to trade on the NASDAQ Global Select Market under the symbol
&#147;TMUS&#148;. The combined company will operate under the name <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The New <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> commitment to building the world&#146;s best broad and deep nationwide 5G network, which will bring lightning-fast speeds to urban areas and underserved rural communities alike, is more critical than
ever, as reliable connectivity has become so important to Americans. With 14 times more capacity in six years than standalone <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has today, the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT>
network will be able to offer unmatched value to consumers, with better service at lower prices. The company will also continue to focus on its commitment to customers and being a force for good. The enhanced scale and financial strength of the
combined company will drive a planned investment of $40&nbsp;billion into its network, business and more over the next three years. Synergies achieved from the integration have the potential to unlock massive scale and unleash at least
$43&nbsp;billion in value for shareholders. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company also announced that with close of the merger, it has successfully completed its long-planned
Chief Executive Officer transition from John Legere to Mike Sievert ahead of schedule. Effective immediately, Sievert will assume the role of CEO of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> Legere, who served as CEO of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> since 2012, built a culture around listening to employees, putting the customer first and shaking up the market with signature <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> moves. During his tenure,
Legere engineered a turnaround of the company as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> completely disrupted the wireless industry and became the fastest growing company in wireless, capturing 80% of the industry&#146;s postpaid phone
growth from 2013 to today. Legere will continue as a member of the Board of Directors for the remainder of his current term, through the Annual Meeting of Shareholders scheduled in June 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;During this extraordinary time, it has become abundantly clear how vital a strong and reliable network is to the world we live in. The New <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> commitment to delivering a transformative broad and deep nationwide 5G network is more important and more needed than ever and what we are building is mission-critical for consumers,&#148; said Mike
Sievert, president and CEO of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> &#147;With this powerful network, the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will deliver real choice and value to wireless and home broadband customers
and double down on all the things customers have always loved about the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier.</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has been changing wireless for good &#151; and now we are going to do it on
a whole new level!&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sievert continued, &#147;All of us at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> owe John an incredible thank you for
everything he&#146;s done to get this company to where we are today. He has changed what it means to be a CEO. Everything that <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has accomplished is the result of his vision for what a different kind of
wireless provider could be. John IS what the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> is all about: advocating for customers at every turn, forcing us to think differently and always driving for more. He has always pushed the boundaries of
what&#146;s possible and pushed us to do the same. His leadership has made us what we are today, and we will take that into the future. Thank you, John, for everything you&#146;ve done for wireless consumers and for our beloved employees! I also
want to thank Marcelo Claure and the entire Sprint leadership team for their hard work to get us to this huge day! We did it!... and I&#146;m looking forward to welcoming Sprint employees into Team Magenta, and to working with you now as a member of
our Board of Directors.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> movement started with <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> saying we were going to shake up wireless &#151; and we did! We eliminated annual service contracts, overages and roaming fees, improved customer service and introduced more value. But there&#146;s more. In
the best and worst of times, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has been here with a dependable network and giving customers <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</FONT></FONT> customer service
they can depend on. Today, when those connections are needed more than ever, we are reinforcing everything we&#146;ve stood for as the supercharged New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile!&#148;</FONT> said John Legere. &#147;You know <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has been all about challenging the status quo &#133; and Sprint has a track record of being a tenacious challenger and a dedicated customer advocate as well. So, with innovation, disruption and obsession
for the customer experience as the foundation that the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> is built on, just imagine what&#146;s to come.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Legere continued, &#147;I&#146;ve been fortunate enough to lead this company for the past seven years, but now it&#146;s time for me to hand the reins over to
Mike Sievert. The Board of Directors and I agree that it makes perfect sense for Mike to assume his leadership role on day one of the new company. He&#146;s ready! I had originally planned to stay on through the end of my contract on April&nbsp;30,
2020, but it makes much more sense to transition this responsibility to Mike today. Mike was the first person I hired at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and I have tremendous faith in his ability to take the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> into its next SUPERCHARGED chapter. Between his leadership, his expanded and talented leadership team and the amazing people at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> the future is SO bright!
The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> that we created started with our employees. Each and every one of them. They are different. They play the game differently, and I love them all. I cannot wait to see what this entire team does
next!&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>THE WORLD&#146;S MOST TRANSFORMATIVE NETWORK </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Strong, dependable network connectivity has never been more critical to customers or to the country. Now the New
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will focus on creating a much-needed transformational nationwide 5G network, driving innovation in the U.S. and bringing wireless access to people throughout the country. This quantum leap forward can
only be achieved by using <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint&#146;s combined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-</FONT> and high-spectrum bands &#151; and only the New <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will have the resources to do it quickly. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">The network will have <B>14 times more capacity in the next six years than
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> alone has today</B>, enabling the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> to leapfrog the competition in network capability and experience. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Customers will have access to <B>average 5G speeds up to eight times faster than current LTE</B> in just a few
years and <B>15 times faster over the next six years</B>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Within six years, the New T-Mobile will provide <B>5G to 99% of the U.S. population</B> and average <B>5G speeds
in excess of 100 Mbps to 90% of the U.S. population</B>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> business plan is built on <B>covering 90% of rural
Americans with average 5G speeds of 50 Mbps</B>, up to two times faster than broadband on average. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;The network is at the core of
everything we do as a business, and it&#146;s critically important for keeping customers connected to each other, their communities and the world,&#148; said Neville Ray, president of Technology at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT>
&#147;The supercharged 5G network that we&#146;ll build as a combined company will be a huge step forward, transforming wireless, fueling innovation and delivering new experiences for customers all across the country that we can&#146;t even imagine
today.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>BETTER PRODUCTS AT LOWER PRICES </B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With
14 times more total capacity in the next six years than <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has today, customers won&#146;t have to choose between great service or low prices &#151; they&#146;ll get both. The New <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will offer free access to 5G and the best rate plans at low prices, now and in the future, so all customers can reap the benefits of a supercharged <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-Carrier</FONT> network
at a great value.&nbsp;And the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has committed to delivering the same or better rate plans for three years, which includes access to 5G, including for prepaid and Lifeline customers.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Backed by that additional capacity, the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> is also taking the fight beyond wireless. By offering an
alternative to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-home</FONT> broadband, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> will provide much-needed competition in home internet to Big Cable, at a time when just under half of the country&#146;s
households have only one or zero options for high-speed broadband. The New T-Mobile&#146;s wireless <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-home</FONT> broadband service will overcome the obstacles to extending traditional wireline access by blanketing
high-capacity coverage over previously difficult to serve areas. Its network will deliver 100+ Mbps speeds for wireless broadband to 90% of the population and offer <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-home</FONT> service to millions of the
country&#146;s households in the next six years. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>A BRAND THAT CUSTOMERS LOVE </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will capitalize on the winning formula it built and double down on what customers love about the brand. It
will also continue to be a force for good, pledging not only to be a bigger company but also a <I>better</I> company. New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> customers should expect everything the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> has ALWAYS stood for: treating customers right, shaking up the status quo and being a force for good. The company will use its network to lift up communities nationwide and bring the benefits of 5G
to as many Americans as possible, and it will continue supporting the programs and causes that matter most to employees and the communities they serve. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">It began with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Connect plan. To address America&#146;s urgent needs around
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> fast-tracked its groundbreaking, lowest-priced plan EVER, launched on March 23. Other initiatives to bring the New
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> newly expanded network capabilities to the customers and communities that can benefit most will launch soon, including the Connecting Heroes Initiative to offer FREE unlimited talk, text and
smartphone data to ALL first responders at ALL public and nonprofit state and local fire, police and EMS agencies; and Project 10Million, delivering free internet access and hardware to 10&nbsp;million households over the next five years. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> customers will also receive industry-leading customer care, and all post-paid customers will have access
to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> award-winning Team of Experts (TEX) model as it expands into every current and planned customer experience center. <B> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>MASSIVE VALUE-CREATION OPPORTUNITY</B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The combined assets
of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint are so complementary that the merger is expected to unlock at least $43&nbsp;billion in synergies for all shareholders. The vast majority of synergies in this deal come from combining
networks, such as reducing redundant cell sites and rapidly deploying spectrum and other technologies more efficiently. The company plans to deliver a seamless, high-quality integration, just as it did with its MetroPCS merger, which was completed a
year earlier than planned. These synergies and our combined scale are expected to put New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> in an enhanced financial position, including significant free-cash flow, margin expansion and strong, flexible
capital structure. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the terms of the transaction, Sprint shareholders will receive a fixed exchange ratio of 0.10256
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> shares for each Sprint share, or the equivalent of approximately 9.75 Sprint shares for each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> share.&nbsp;As previously announced, per a separate
arrangement, SoftBank Group Corp. surrendered approximately 48.8&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> shares acquired in the merger to New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> immediately following the closing of
the transaction, making SoftBank&#146;s effective ratio 11.31 Sprint shares per <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> share. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Effective at the
beginning of today&#146;s trading session, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will trade on the NASDAQ on a combined basis under the ticker symbol &#147;TMUS.&#148; The Sprint shares will no longer trade on the New York Stock Exchange.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">PJT Partners and Goldman Sachs acted as financial advisors to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> Wachtell, Lipton, Rosen&nbsp;&amp; Katz
provided legal counsel to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Deutsche Telekom. Evercore acted as financial advisor to the committee of independent directors of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Latham&nbsp;&amp;
Watkins provided legal counsel to the committee of independent directors. Morgan Stanley served as a financial advisor to Deutsche Telekom. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Raine
Group LLC acted as lead financial advisor to Sprint. J.P. Morgan also acted as a financial advisor to Sprint. Morrison&nbsp;&amp; Foerster LLP provided legal counsel to Sprint and SoftBank. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> U.S. Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) is America&#146;s supercharged <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier,</FONT> delivering an advanced 4G LTE and transformative&nbsp;nationwide 5G network that will offer
reliable connectivity for all. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> customers benefit from its unmatched combination of value and quality, unwavering obsession with offering them the best possible service experience and
undisputable drive for disruption that creates competition and innovation in wireless and beyond. Based in Bellevue, Wash., <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> provides services through its subsidiaries and operates its flagship brands,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Metro by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint. For more information please visit: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">http://www.t-mobile.com.</FONT> </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
